[TEXT]   Welcome to Rocket Pictures Studios.  It's everything a Hollywood studio should be:  it has a bold, impressive gate; the grounds of the lot extending to the north are lined with rows of pale hangar-like soundstage buildings and ceramic-roofed bungalows; there's a staggering abundance of motorhomes; it has its own watertower; and it's not actually in Hollywood at all.
  (This last is demonstrated by the fact that there are one- and two-story shopping plazas and office buildings stretching as far as the eye can see instead of souvenir shops and T-shirt stands.)
